Home

For every inference sentence of a given image, we add a negative inference sentence that is of the same inference type but is taken from a different image. The first 5000 or so examples of these "positive/negative inference statements" from the test dataset are shown in the table below. We used UNITER pretrained model, Roberta text embedder, and Roberta tokenizer.

Our model scored an 60.21% accuracy on the test data. Other evaluation metrics are as follows:

  • precision (PPV): 66.10%
  • recall (TPR): 38.42%
  • NPV: 56.59%
  • specificity (TNR): 80.29%
The examples that are classified as false positives are highlighted in green, and the examples that are classified as false negatives are highlighted in pink
